When TripsInHand fold force

//best hands - AA double suited and two big connectors

when (hand =AsuitedAsuited and suitsInHand =2 and not TwoPairInHand and not hand =9 and lowCardsInHand =1) 

	when raises >=0 raisepot force


//AA and a big pair

when (hand =AAKK or hand =AAQQ or hand =AAJJ or hand =AATT)

	when raises <2 call force	
	when raises >=2 and betsize <11 call force


//Big Rundown hands (Ace through Ten)

when ((hand =A and not hand =9 and lowCardsInHand =1) or (lowcardsinhand =0 and not hand =9))  and not hand =AA

	when raises =0 and bets =0 and stilltoact <=4 and not insmallblind and not inbigblind raisepot force
	when raises =0 and bets =0 call force
	when raises <2 call force

//Middle Rundown hands

when (hand =6789 or hand =789T or hand =89TJ or hand =9TJQ)

	when raises =0 and bets =0 and stilltoact <=3 and not insmallblind and not inbigblind raisepot force
	when raises =0 and bets =0 call force
	when raises =1 and betsize <5 call force


//Small Rundown Hands

when (hand =5678 or hand =4567 or hand =3456)

	when raises =0 and bets =0 and stilltoact <=3 and not insmallblind and not inbigblind and random <33 raisepot force
	when raises =0 and bets =0 call force
	when raises =1 and betsize <5 call force


//Three Rundown cards with a pair

when (hand =A223 or hand =2234 or hand =A233 or hand =3345 or hand =3445 or hand =4456 or

      hand =9TTJ or hand =TTJQ or hand =9TJJ or hand =TJJQ or hand =JJQK)

	when lowcardsinhand <2 and raises =0 and bets =0 and stilltoact <=3 and not insmallblind and not inbigblind raisepot force
	when raises =0 call force
	when raises =1 and betsize <5 call force


//Ace suited big rundown hands with two gaps

	when raises =0 and bets =0 and stilltoact <=3 and not insmallblind and not inbigblind raisepot force
	when raises =0 and bets =0 call force
	when raises <2 call force

      hand =4678 or hand =5679 or hand =5689 or hand =5789 or hand =678T or hand =679T or hand =689T or hand =789J or
      hand =78TJ or hand =79TJ or hand =89tQ or hand =89JQ or hand =8TJQ or hand =9TJk or hand =9TQK or hand =9JQK)

	when raises =0 and bets =0 and folds >1 and not lastcallerposition =3 and stilltoact <=3 and not insmallblind and not inbigblind and random <50 raisepot force
	when raises =0 and bets =0 call force
	when raises =1 and lowcardsinhand <2 and betsize <6 call force
	when raises =1 and betsize <5 call force

	when raises =0 and stilltoact <4 call force
	when raises =1 and calls >1 and betsize <4 call forcE

//Aces or Kings or AK double suited

when (hand =AA or hand =KK or hand =AsuitedQQ or (hand =AsuitedKsuited and not hand =AsKs and not hand =AcKc and not hand =AhKh and not hand =AdKd))

	when stacksize <10 raisemax force
	when opponentsAtTable <6 and (hand =AAsuited or hand =KKsuited) and InButton and raises =0 and bets =0 and calls =0 raisepot force
	when raises =0 and bets =0 and stilltoact <=3 and not insmallblind and not inbigblind raisepot  force
	when raises >0 and (hand =AA) and (insmallblind or inbigblind) and calls =0 call force
	when raises >0 and (hand =AA) and (insmallblind or inbigblind) and calls >0 raisepot force
	when raises >=0 and (hand =AA) raisepot force
	when hand =KK and not insmallblind and not inbigblind and raises =0 and bets =0 raisepot force
	when hand =kk and raises <=1 call force
	when raises <=1 and betsize <6 call force

//Double Suited with an Ace

when suitsInHand =2 and not pairinhand and 
(hand = A suited K suited) and ((hand = A d and   (not hand = 2 d and not hand = 3 d and not hand = 4 d and not hand = 5 d and not hand = 6 d and not hand = 7 d and not  
                                                   hand = 8 d and not hand = 9 d and not hand = T d and not hand = J d and not hand = Q d)) or
                              (hand = A s and   (not hand = 2 s and not hand = 3 s and not hand = 4 s and not hand = 5 s and not hand = 6 s and not hand = 7 s and not  
                                                   hand = 8 s and not hand = 9 s and not hand = T s and not hand = J s and not hand = Q s)) or
			      (hand = A c and   (not hand = 2 c and not hand = 3 c and not hand = 4 c and not hand = 5 c and not hand = 6 c and not hand = 7 c and not  
                                                   hand = 8 c and not hand = 9 c and not hand = T c and not hand = J c and not hand = Q c)) or
			      (hand = A h and   (not hand = 2 h and not hand = 3 h and not hand = 4 h and not hand = 5 h and not hand = 6 h and not hand = 7 h and not  
                                                   hand = 8 h and not hand = 9 h and not hand = T h and not hand = J h and not hand = Q h)))
	when raises =0 call force
	when raises =1 and betsize <=3 call force
	when others fold

	when (flushPossible or straightPossible) and opponents =1 and HaveTopSet call force
	when straightpossible and not havestraight and havestraightdraw and not havebottomset raisepot force
	when (flushPossible or straightPossible) and betsize >4 and not haveFlush and not HaveStraight fold force
	when (flushPossible or straightPossible) and betsize <=4 and not haveFlush and not HaveStraight and opponents =1 and position =last and raises =0 and bets =0 raisepot force
	when (flushPossible or straightPossible) and betsize <=4 and not haveFlush and not HaveStraight call force
	when HaveStraightDraw and not HaveInsideStraightDraw and not FlushPossible and raises=0 and not position =first and opponents <3 raisepot force
	when HaveStraightDraw and not HaveInsideStraightDraw and not FlushPossible call force
	when HaveBottomSet and opponents >2 and raises >1 fold force
        when haveFlush raisepot force
	when haveset and not havebottomset and havenutflushdraw raisepot force
        when havebottomset and opponents >1 and not position =last and suitsonboard =2 and raises =0 and bets =0 call force
	when raises <=2 and not flushPossible and not straightPossible raisepot force
	when raises <2 and position =first and not flushPossible call force
	when raises =0 and not position =first and not flushPossible raisepot force
	when raises =1 and not flushPossible call force
	when botslastaction =raise and (raises =1 or bets =1)  call force

//Top Two Pair situations

when HaveTopTwoPair and opponents >2 and not havefullhouse and not haveflush and not havestraight and not haveset and not havetrips

	when (pairOnBoard or flushPossible or StraightPossible) and not haveFlush and not HaveStraight fold force
	when raises =0 and suitsonBoard =3 bet 25% force
	when raises =0 call force
	when raises =1 and betsize <50% potsize call force
	when botslastaction =raise and (raises =1 or bets =1)  call force
	when others fold
	
when HaveTopTwoPair and opponents <=2 and not haveflush and not havestraight and not haveset and not havetrips

	when opponents =1 and not flushpossible and raises =0 and bets =0 bet 75% force
	when (pairOnBoard or flushPossible or StraightPossible) and not haveFlush and not HaveStraight fold force
	when not straightpossible and suitsonboard =2 and random <50 raisepot force
	when not straightpossible and suitsonboard =2 and bets =0 and raises =0 call force
	when not straightpossible and suitsonboard =3 raisepot force
	when raises =0 and position =last raisepot force
	when raises =0 and bets =0 and suitsonboard =3 and not straightpossible and opponents <=2 raisepot force
	when raises =0 and not position =last call force
	when raises =1 and calls <2 and opponents <3 and betsize <=50% potsize and betsize <5 call force
	when botslastaction =raise and (raises =1 or bets =1)  call force
	when others fold

//TwoPair w/ Top Pair

when haveTwoPair and haveTopPair and not flushPossible and not straightPossible and not paironboard and not haveset and not havetrips
	when havenutflushdraw raisepot force
	when raises =0 and bets =0 and opponents =1 and position =last raisepot force
	when raises =0 and bets =0 call force
	when (raises =1 or bets =1) and opponents <=2 and betsize <=2 call force

  when opponents >1 and suitsonboard <3 and betsize >25% potsize fold force
  when not position =last and raises =0 and bets =0 call force

//when have overpair

when botraisedbeforeflop and (hand =AA or hand =KK) and not havestraight and not haveflush and not havefullhouse and not haveset and not havetrips
  when position =first and (flushpossible or straightpossible) and raises =0 and bets =0 call force
  when (flushpossible or straightpossible) and (raises =1 or bets =1) and betsize >=40% potsize fold force

//flush drawing

when haveflushdraw and not haveflush and not haveset and not havetrips and not havestraight and not havefullhouse and not havequads and not havetwopair
  when havenutflushdraw and not paironboard and position =last and raises =0 and bets =0 bet 70% force
  when (havetoppair or haveoverpair) and havenutflushdraw and not paironboard raisepot force
  when opponents >2 and not havenutflushdraw and not have2ndnutflushdraw and not have3rdnutflushdraw fold force
  when opponents >2 and not position =last and not (havenutflushdraw or have2ndnutflushdraw) and betsize >50% potsize fold force
  when not (havenutflushdraw or have2ndnutflushdraw) and not paironboard and not BotsLastAction =raise and raises >1 fold force
  when botslastaction =raise and raises =1 and not havenutflushdraw and not have2ndnutflushdraw and havestraightdraw and opponents =1 call force

//straightdrawing

when havestraightdraw and not havestraight and not haveflush and not havenutflushdraw and not havefullhouse and not havequads and not haveset
  when havenutstraightdraw and suitsonboard =3 and havetoppair raisepot force
  when opponents >1 and haveinsidestraightdraw and not have10outstraightdraw and not have2ndnutflushdraw and raises =0 and bets =0 call force
  when position =first and opponents >1 and not havenutstraightdraw and raises =0 and bets =0 call force

//when bot raised pre-flop with KK

when hand =KK and BotRaisedBeforeFlop
  when opponents <=2 and suitsonboard =3 and havestraightdraw and not haveinsidestraightdraw raisepot force
  when position =last and raises =0 and bets =0 and paironboard and lowcardsonboard =2 raisepot force

when hand =kk
  when opponents =1 and not straightpossible and suitsonboard =3 and (betsize <=50% potsize or betsize <5) call force

//Heads Up with a Pre-Flop Raise

when hand =AA and BotRaisedBeforeFlop
  when opponents =1 and position =first and not havestraightdraw and not haveflushdraw and not paironboard and not havetrips and not haveset and betsize >=50% potsize fold force
  when not havestraightdraw and not haveflushdraw and suitsonboard <3 and not paironboard and not havetrips and not haveset and betsize >=30% potsize fold force
  when opponents =1 and potsize >25 and stacksize <35 and not flushpossible and not straightpossible raisepot force
  when opponents =2 and suitsonboard =3 and not straightpossible and not position =first and random <60 bet 65% force

when (RaisesBeforeFlop or BotRaisedBeforeFlop) and opponents =1 and position =last and checks =1 and raises =0 and bets =0
  when ((haveTopPair and havebestkicker) or haveTopTwoPair or (Have16OutStraightDraw or Have12OutStraightDraw) or haveNutStraight or haveTrips) and not flushpossible raisepot force
  when (((haveStraightDraw and not haveInsideStraightDraw) and not flushpossible) or havenutflush or have2ndnutflush or havenutflushdraw)  raisepot force
  when hand =KK and not straightpossible and suitsonboard =3 and raises =0 and bets =0 raisepot force

when (RaisesBeforeFlop or BotRaisedBeforeFlop) and opponents =1 and position =first
  when not havetwopair and not haveset and not havetrips and not havestraight and not haveflush and not havefullhouse and not havequads and not (havestraightdraw and not haveinsidestraightdraw) and not havenutflushdraw and not have2ndnutflushdraw and not hand =AA and raises =0 and bets =0 call force
    when hand =KK and not straightpossible and suitsonboard =3 and raises =0 and bets =0 raisepot force
    when hand =KK and not straightpossible and suitsonboard =3 and (raises =1 or bets =1) raisehalfpot force

//heads up with no preflop raise last to act

when opponents =1 and position =last
  when raises =0 and bets =0 and haveTopPair and haveTwoPair and not paironboard and not straightpossible and not flushPossible raisepot force
  when raises =0 and bets =0 and not RaisesBeforeFlop and not BotRaisedbeforeFlop and random <66 raisepot force

when opponents <=2 and position =last
  when hand =AA and raises =0 and bets =0 and haveTopPair and haveTwoPair and not straightpossible and not flushPossible raisepot force

//More bluffing

when position =last and (RaisesBeforeFlop or BotRaisedBeforeFlop) and opponents <2
  when raises =0 and bets =0 and (HaveBestOverpairOrBetter or (havetoppair and overcards >1) or (havenutstraightdraw and not haveinsidestraightdraw) or havenutflushdraw or have2ndnutflushdraw) and random <65 raisepot force

//folding

when havepair and not pairinhand
  when not havetwopair and not haveset and not havetrips and not havestraight and not haveflush and not havefullhouse and not havequads and not havestraightdraw and not haveflushdraw fold force

turn

When TotalInvested > 140% StackSize  RaiseMax force

when havenothing and opponents >2 and not position =last fold force

when havenutflush and paironboard and raises =0 and bets =0 call force
when havenutflush and not paironboard bet 75% force
when have2ndnutflush and paironboard and raises =0 and bets =0 and position =last bet 65% force
when have2ndnutflush and paironboard and raises =0 and bets =0 call force
when have2ndnutflush and paironboard and (raises =1 or bets =1) and betsize <=50% potsize call force

when havestraight and not haveflush and not havefullhouse and not havequads and not haveset and not havetrips and not (havenutflushdraw or have2ndnutflushdraw)
  when not havenutstraight and suitsonboard <3 and opponents >2 and betsize >50% potsize fold force
  when not havenutstraight and suitsonboard <3 and raises =0 and bets =0 call force

when havetrips and not havequads and not havefullhouse and not flushpossible
  when opponents >1 and not position =last and not havebestkicker and not have2ndbestkicker and not have3rdbestkicker and raises =0 and bets =0 call force
  when opponents >1 and not position =last and not havebestkicker and not have2ndbestkicker and not have3rdbestkicker and (raises =1 or bets =1) and betsize <=100% potsize and havenutstraightdraw  call force

	when (flushPossible or straightPossible) and betsize <=4 and not haveFlush and not HaveStraight call force
	when (havenutflushdraw or have2ndnutflushdraw) call force
	when HaveStraightDraw and not HaveInsideStraightDraw and not FlushPossible and raises=0 and not position =first and opponents <3 raisepot force
	when HaveStraightDraw and not HaveInsideStraightDraw and not FlushPossible call force
	when HaveBottomSet and opponents >2 and raises >1 fold force
	when haveflush and not havenutflush and not have2ndnutflush and not have3rdnutflush and not have4thnutflush and opponents >2 and raises =0 and bets =0 call force
        when haveFlush raisepot force
	when haveset and not havebottomset and havenutflushdraw raisepot force
	when raises <2 and position =first call force
	when raises =0 and not position =first bet 60% force
	when raises =1 call force
	when botslastaction =raise and (raises =1 or bets =1)  call force

  when haveflushdraw and havenutstraightdraw and opponents <=2 and raises =0 and bets =0 raisepot force
  when haveflushdraw and havenutstraightdraw and opponents <=2 and (raises =1 or bets =1) call force

//flush drawing

when haveflushdraw and not haveflush and not haveset and not havetrips and not havestraight and not havefullhouse and not havequads and not havetwopair
  when opponents >2 and not (havenutflushdraw or have2ndnutflushdraw or have3rdnutflushdraw) fold force
  when opponents >2 and not position =last and not (havenutflushdraw or have2ndnutflushdraw) and betsize >50% potsize fold force
  when not (havenutflushdraw or have2ndnutflushdraw) and not paironboard and raises >1 fold force

  when position =first and opponents >1 and not havenutstraightdraw and raises =0 and bets =0 call force
  when opponents >1 and raises =0 and bets =0 call force

//Bluffing and Semi-bluffing

when opponents =1 and botRaisedBeforeFlop
  when (OpponentCalledOnFlop or CalledOnFlop) and not havetwopair and not havestraight and not haveflush and not havefullhouse and not havequads and not havenutflushdraw and not have2ndnutflushdraw and not haveset and not havetrips and not havenutstraightdraw and position =first and raises =0 and bets =0 call force
  when not pairOnBoard and not FlushPossible and not StraightPossible and HaveOverPair and hand =AA raisepot force

when opponents =1 and RaisesBeforeFlop and position =last
  when raises =0 and bets =0 and paironboard and not flushpossible and not straightPossible and haveOverpair and NoBettingOnFlop raisepot force
  when (raises =1 or bets =1) and paironboard and not flushpossible and not straightPossible and haveOverpair and (hand = TT or hand =JJ or hand =QQ or hand =KK or hand =AA) and nobettingonflop and betsize <=50% potsize call force

when opponents =1 and position =last
when raises =0 and bets =0 and haveTopPair and haveTwoPair and not paironboard and not straightpossible and not flushPossible raisepot force
when (raises =1 or bets =1) and haveToptwoPair and not paironboard and not straightpossible and not flushPossible and not RaisesOnFlop call force

when (havenutstraightdraw and not haveInsideStraightDraw and not haveStraight) and haveflushdraw and opponents <=2
  when raises =0 and bets =0 raisepot force
  when (raises =1 or bets =1) and opponents =1 and position =last and not paironboard call force

when not RaisesBeforeFlop and not BotRaisedBeforeFlop and opponents <3
  when position =last and raises =0 and bets =0 bet 60% force

//slow-down play

when botraisedbeforeflop and BotRaisedOnFlop and OpponentCalledOnFlop
  when hand =AA and position =last and raises =0 and bets =0 and paironboard call force
  when opponents =1 and position =first and not havetoppair and not havetwopair and not havetrips and not haveset and not havestraight and not haveflush and not havefullhouse and not havequads and not haveflushdraw and not (havenutstraightdraw and not haveinsidestraightdraw)
       and raises =0 and bets =0 call force

  when flushpossible and not haveflush and not havefullhouse and not havetrips and not haveset and raises =0 and bets =0 call force
  when flushpossible and not haveflush and not havefullhouse and not havetrips and not haveset and betsize > 33% potsize fold force

river

When TotalInvested > 140% StackSize  RaiseMax force

when havenothing and opponents >2 and not position =last fold force

when havefullhouse and not havequads
  when NutFullHouseOrFourOfAKind <3 bet 70% force  
  when NutFullHouseOrFourOfAKind >3 and not raisesbeforeflop and not BotRaisedBeforeFlop and nobettingonflop and nobettingonturn and raises =0 and bets =0 bet 66% force
  when NutFullHouseOrFourOfAKind >3 and not raisesbeforeflop and not BotRaisedBeforeFlop and nobettingonflop and nobettingonturn and (raises =1 or bets =1) call force

when haveflush and not havefullhouse
  when havenutflush and not paironboard bet 70% force
  when havenutflush and paironboard and nobettingonflop and nobettingonturn and raises =0 and bets =0 bet 50% force
  when havenutflush and paironboard and nobettingonflop and nobettingonturn and betsize <=50% potsize call force
  when have2ndnutflush and not paironboard and opponents =1 and position =first bet 60% force
  when have2ndnutflush and not paironboard and opponents =1 and position =last and raises =0 and bets =0 bet 66% force
  when have2ndnutflush and not paironboard and opponents =1 and position =last and (raises =1 or bets =1) call force
  
when havestraight and not haveflush and not havefullhouse and not havequads
  when (raises =1 or bets =1) and have2ndnutstraight and totalinvested >14 and stacksize <26 and not flushpossible and not paironboard call force
  when flushpossible and not haveflush and havenutstraight and (betsize <=50% potsize or betsize <5) call force
  when not flushpossible and not havenutstraight and not nobettingonturn and opponents >1 and betsize >50% potsize fold force
  when paironboard and position =last and raises =0 and bets =0 call force

when havetwopair and not haveset and not havetrips and not haveflush and not havestraight and not havefullhouse and not havequads
  when (straightpossible or flushpossible) and position =first and raises =0 and bets =0 call force

  when havetwopair and not havetoptwopair and not haveset and not havetrips and betsize >=50% potsize fold force
